## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (ODE rate laws for concentration vs time)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a concentration A(t), which is the standard object modeled by chemical kinetics rate laws. With only t and A available, the most likely relationships are autonomous rate laws dA_dt = f(A) (reaction-order, reversible, autocatalytic) and/or time-dependent effective rate constants dA_dt = f(t, A) (catalyst/temperature programs, deactivation, forcing).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption when reagent is in excess or surface-limited)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular with one reactant effectively equal to A)
- n-th order power-law kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical reaction order, chain reactions/fractional order)
- Linear source + sink: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (production plus first-order loss; chemostat-like balance)
- Approach to equilibrium (linear relaxation): dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (relaxation toward equilibrium concentration c1)
- Reversible 2-state surrogate (nonlinear equilibrium approach): dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * (c2 - A) (A interconverts with a pool of total c2)
- Autocatalytic/Verhulst-type rate form: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating formation with depletion/finite capacity)
- Inhibited/limited rate (rational): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + A) (effective saturation/inhibition in the disappearance rate)
- Time-varying first-order (exponential deactivation): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (rate constant decays over time due to catalyst decay or quench)
- Time-varying first-order (ramp/program): dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + c2 * t) * A (linearly changing conditions producing a time-dependent rate constant)
- Oscillatory forcing of rate: dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (periodic modulation of kinetics by external cycling)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Straight line in dA_dt vs A through origin suggests first-order: dA_dt proportional to A.
- Curvature in log(-dA_dt) vs log(A) suggests power-law order: dA_dt proportional to A**c.
- Nonzero intercept in dA_dt vs A suggests concurrent source term: dA_dt = c0 - c1*A.
- Sign change of dA_dt around a specific A indicates an equilibrium point: factors like (A - c1) or (c1 - A).
- Rapid initial change that slows strongly as A grows can indicate rational limitation/inhibition: A/(c1 + A) type structure.
- If trajectories with similar A but different t have different dA_dt, include an explicit time-dependent rate factor k(t) multiplying A or A**c.
- Systematic slowing over time at fixed A suggests deactivation via exp(-c*t) or other monotone k(t) decay.
- Periodic wiggles in residuals vs t suggest adding sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) modulation to an otherwise autonomous rate law.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK13)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidate formulas: 52

GT is a fixed function of **A only** (no t-dependence):
\[
f(A)= -0.23236613283613416\,A + 0.395876449251558\,\sin(0.5265654762365851\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must be reducible (by choosing its free constants) to **(linear in A) + (single sine in A with zero phase shift)**, with **no extra terms** (no exp/log/rational/Abs/polynomial powers), and must be **independent of t** for all t.

---

### 1. `c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7`
To match GT, exp and log terms must vanish: set `c0=0`, `c5=0`. Then we have `c2*sin(A*c3+c4)+c7`. But GT also has a linear `-0.232...*A` term; there is no linear term here. Cannot match.

### 2. `A*c0/(A + c1) + A**c2*c3 + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6)`
Need linear term and sine term only. The rational `A*c0/(A+c1)` cannot become exactly linear in A for all A unless it is identically 0 (set `c0=0`) or becomes constant-like (not linear). If `c0=0`, then need `A**c2*c3` to be linear: set `c2=1`, `c3=-0.232...`. Sine: set `c4=0.395876...`, `c5=0.526565...`, and phase `c6=0`. This works. **Matches.**

### 3. `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3) + c4`
Set `c4=0` (GT has no constant offset). Need `A*c0` to be `-0.232...A` so `c0=-0.232366...`. Need sine amplitude/frequency and zero phase: `c1=0.395876...`, `c2=0.526565...`, `c3=0`. Works. **Matches.**

### 4. `A*c0 + c1*(A + c2)**3 + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5)`
Cubic term must vanish: set `c1=0`. Then it reduces to `A*c0 + c3*sin(A*c4+c5)`; choose `c0=-0.232...`, `c3=0.395876...`, `c4=0.526565...`, `c5=0`. **Matches.**

### 5. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4)`
GT has no t dependence. For `A*c0*exp(c1*t)` to be t-independent for all t, need `c1=0` so `exp(0)=1`. Then it becomes `A*c0 + c2*sin(A*c3+c4)`; choose `c0=-0.232...`, `c2=0.395876...`, `c3=0.526565...`, `c4=0`. **Matches.**

### 6. `A*c0 + A*c1*(c2 + t)**c3 + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6)`
To remove t dependence, set `c1=0`. Then same as linear + sine; pick constants as above with `c0=-0.232...`, `c4=0.395876...`, `c5=0.526565...`, `c6=0`. **Matches.**

### 7. `c0*Abs(A)**c1 + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4)`
No explicit linear `A` term unless `Abs(A)**c1` becomes proportional to `A` for all real A. `Abs(A)` cannot equal `A` on negative A, so cannot represent `-0.232...A` globally. If you try to kill it (`c0=0`), then no linear term remains. Cannot match.

### 8. `c0*Abs(A) + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`
Same issue: `Abs(A)` cannot equal `A` for all A. If `c0=0`, lose linear term. Cannot match.

### 9. `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`
Exactly the GT form (linear + sine). Choose `c0=-0.232366...`, `c1=0.395876...`, `c2=0.526565...`, `c3=0`. **Matches.**

### 10. `A*c0 + c1*Abs(A)**c2 + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5)`

### 11. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5)`

Remove both exp terms: set `c1=0`, `c6=0`. Then linear + sine; choose constants. **Matches.**

### 41. `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1/sqrt(c2 + t) + A*c3 + A*c4/sqrt(c2 + t) + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)`
Remove all non-GT terms: set `c0=0`, `c1=0`, `c4=0`. Then `A*c3 + c5*sin(...)`; choose `c3=-0.232...`, `c5=0.395876...`, `c6=0.526565...`, `c7=0`. **Matches.**

### 42. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5 + c6*log(A*c7 + 1)`
Kill quadratic, constant, log: set `c0=0`, `c5=0`, `c6=0`. Then linear + sine; choose constants. **Matches.**

### 43. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6*exp(A*c7) + c8/(A*c2 + c3) + c9`
Even if kill log/exp/quadratic (`c4=0,c6=0,c0=0`), remaining rational terms `A*c1/(A*c2+c3)+c8/(A*c2+c3)+c9` cannot become exactly linear in A for all A unless you set `c1=c8=0`, leaving constant `c9` only. No sine term either unless introduced (none). Cannot match.

### 44. `A*c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5) + c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8`
Kill exp/log/constant: set `c1=0`, `c6=0`, `c8=0`. Then linear + sine; choose constants. **Matches.**

### 45. (many terms)/(A + c1) with logs
To match GT (no denominator), would need to eliminate the entire division effect. Setting numerator terms to cancel denominator for all A is not possible while also producing a pure linear + sine (and logs would need removal). If set all log coefficients 0 and polynomial coefficients 0, expression becomes 0, losing GT. Cannot match.

### 46. `A + c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6*exp(A*c7) + c8`
There is a fixed `A` term with coefficient 1 that cannot be removed. GT’s linear coefficient is `-0.232...`, not 1, and there’s no way to change that coefficient since it’s not parameterized. Cannot match.

### 47. `A*c0/(A + c1) + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7*sin(c8 + c9*t)`
To remove t dependence, set `c7=0`. Remove log: `c5=0`. Then left with rational + sine; but no linear term unless rational can be linear (it can’t, except 0). If set `c0=0`, no linear term. Cannot match.

### 48. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5*exp(A*c6) + c7`
Kill quadratic, exp, constant: set `c0=0`, `c5=0`, `c7=0`. Then linear + sine; choose constants. **Matches.**

### 49. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8/(A*c2 + c3) + c9`
Kill exp/log and rational extras: set `c4=0`, `c6=0`, `c1=0`, `c8=0`, `c9=0`. Then only `A*c0` remains (no sine). Cannot match.

### 50. `c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7*exp(A*c8) + c9`
Kill exp/log: set `c0=0`, `c5=0`, `c7=0`. Then `c2*sin(...)+c9`. Need linear term; none. Cannot match.

### 51. `c0*sin(A*c1 + c2) + c3*log(A*c4 + 1)`
Kill log: `c3=0`. Then only sine; no linear term. Cannot match.

### 52. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6) + c7*exp(A*c8) + c9`
Kill rational and exp and constant: set `c1=0`, `c7=0`, `c9=0`. Then linear + sine; choose `c0=-0.232...`, `c4=0.395876...`, `c5=0.526565...`, `c6=0`. **Matches.**
